  276     -- Signals
  277     SIGNAL addr_A_unsigned                  : unsigned(9 DOWNTO 0);  -- ufix10
  278     SIGNAL convertA_out1                    : unsigned(15 DOWNTO 0);  -- uint16
  279     SIGNAL ram_data_A_out1                  : unsigned(15 DOWNTO 0);  -- uint16
  280     SIGNAL And_out1                         : std_logic;
  281     SIGNAL din_A_signed                     : signed(31 DOWNTO 0);  -- sfix32_En28
  282     SIGNAL din_B_signed                     : signed(31 DOWNTO 0);  -- sfix32_En28
  283     SIGNAL addr_B_unsigned                  : unsigned(9 DOWNTO 0);  -- ufix10
  284     SIGNAL convertB_out1                    : unsigned(15 DOWNTO 0);  -- uint16
  285     SIGNAL switch_A_out1                    : vector_of_signed32(0 TO 1023);  -- sfix32_En28 [1024]
  286     SIGNAL wr_port1_out1                    : vector_of_signed32(0 TO 1023);  -- sfix32_En28 [1024]
  287     SIGNAL ram_out1                         : vector_of_signed32(0 TO 1023);  -- sfix32_En28 [1024]
  288     SIGNAL wr_port_out1                     : vector_of_signed32(0 TO 1023);  -- sfix32_En28 [1024]
  289     SIGNAL switch_A2_out1                   : vector_of_signed32(0 TO 1023);  -- sfix32_En28 [1024]
  290     SIGNAL switch_B_out1                    : vector_of_signed32(0 TO 1023);  -- sfix32_En28 [1024]
  291     SIGNAL select_A_idx                     : unsigned(16 DOWNTO 0);  -- ufix17
  292     SIGNAL select_A_sub_cast                : signed(31 DOWNTO 0);  -- int32
  293     SIGNAL select_A_out1                    : signed(31 DOWNTO 0);  -- sfix32_En28
  294     SIGNAL Data_Type_Conversion_Inherited_A_out1 : std_logic_vector(31 DOWNTO 0);  -- ufix32
  295     SIGNAL ram_data_B_out1                  : unsigned(15 DOWNTO 0);  -- uint16
  296     SIGNAL select_B_idx                     : unsigned(16 DOWNTO 0);  -- ufix17
  297     SIGNAL select_B_sub_cast                : signed(31 DOWNTO 0);  -- int32
  298     SIGNAL select_B_out1                    : signed(31 DOWNTO 0);  -- sfix32_En28
  299     SIGNAL Data_Type_Conversion_Inherited_B_out1 : std_logic_vector(31 DOWNTO 0);  -- ufix32

  301   BEGIN
  302     -- <S13>/Data Type Conversion Inherited A
  303     u_Data_Type_Conversion_Inherited_A : pFIR_HPF_testing_and_analysis_Data_Type_Conversion_Inherited_A
  304       PORT MAP( u => std_logic_vector(select_A_out1),  -- sfix32_En28
  305                 y => Data_Type_Conversion_Inherited_A_out1  -- sfix32_En28
  306                 );
  307   
  308     -- <S13>/Data Type Conversion Inherited B
  309     u_Data_Type_Conversion_Inherited_B : pFIR_HPF_testing_and_analysis_Data_Type_Conversion_Inherited_B
  310       PORT MAP( u => std_logic_vector(select_B_out1),  -- sfix32_En28
  311                 y => Data_Type_Conversion_Inherited_B_out1  -- sfix32_En28
  312                 );
  313   
  314     -- <S13>/Signal SpecificationA
  315     addr_A_unsigned <= unsigned(addr_A);
  316   
  317     -- <S13>/convertA
  318     convertA_out1 <= resize(addr_A_unsigned, 16);
  319   
  320     -- <S13>/ram_data_A
  321     ram_data_A_process : PROCESS (clk, reset)
  322     BEGIN
  323       IF reset = '1' THEN
  324         ram_data_A_out1 <= to_unsigned(16#0000#, 16);
  325       ELSIF rising_edge(clk) THEN
  326         IF enb_1_2_0 = '1' THEN
  327           ram_data_A_out1 <= convertA_out1;
  328         END IF;
  329       END IF;
  330     END PROCESS ram_data_A_process;
  331

  334     And_out1 <= we_A OR we_B;
  335   
  336     din_A_signed <= signed(din_A);
  337   
  338     din_B_signed <= signed(din_B);

 6509     -- <S13>/ram
 6510     ram_process : PROCESS (clk, reset)
 6511     BEGIN
 6512       IF reset = '1' THEN
 6513         ram_out1 <= ram_data;
 6514       ELSIF rising_edge(clk) THEN
 6515         IF enb_1_2_0 = '1' THEN
 6516           ram_out1 <= switch_B_out1;
 6517         END IF;
 6518       END IF;
 6519     END PROCESS ram_process;
 6520   
 6521   
 6522     -- <S13>/select_A
 6523     select_A_idx <= resize(ram_data_A_out1, 17) + to_unsigned(16#00001#, 17);
 6524     select_A_sub_cast <= signed(resize(select_A_idx, 32));
 6525   
 6526     select_A_out1 <= ram_out1(to_integer(select_A_sub_cast - 1)) WHEN select_A_idx <= to_unsigned(16#003FF#, 17) ELSE
 6527         ram_out1(1023);

 6531     BEGIN
 6532       IF reset = '1' THEN
 6533         ram_data_B_out1 <= to_unsigned(16#0000#, 16);
 6534       ELSIF rising_edge(clk) THEN
 6535         IF enb_1_2_0 = '1' THEN
 6536           ram_data_B_out1 <= convertB_out1;
 6537         END IF;
 6538       END IF;
 6539     END PROCESS ram_data_B_process;
 6540   
 6541

 6547         ram_out1(1023);
